<h1 style="padding:0px; margin:20px 0px 10px; line-height:43.2000007629395px; font-size:24px">
一。分布式环境搭建</h1>
<p style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; letter-spacing:0.5px; font-size:12.5px">

<span id="OSC_h2_2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"></span>
<h2 style="padding:0px; margin:20px 0px 10px; line-height:36px; font-size:20px">1.<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">在</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">master</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">主控机安装</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">HBase</span></h2>

<h3 style="padding:0px; margin:15px 0px 10px; line-height:28.7999992370605px; font-size:16px">

<h2 style="padding:0px; margin:20px 0px 10px; line-height:36px; font-size:20px">7.<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">查询条目</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">get </span></h2>
<p style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; letter-spacing:0.5px; font-size:12.5px">
<a target="_blank" href="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163602_lcgi_256028.png" rel="nofollow" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:rgb(255,131,115); outline:0px; font-size:12px"><img src="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163602_lcgi_256028.png" alt="" style="padding:5px; margin:10px 0px; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:640px; background:rgb(244,247,249)"></a></p>
<span id="OSC_h2_19" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"></span>
<h2 style="padding:0px; margin:20px 0px 10px; line-height:36px; font-size:20px">8.<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">更新条目</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">put</span></h2>
<p style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; letter-spacing:0.5px; font-size:12.5px">
<a target="_blank" href="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163611_BNas_256028.png" rel="nofollow" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:rgb(255,131,115); outline:0px; font-size:12px"><img src="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163611_BNas_256028.png" alt="" style="padding:5px; margin:10px 0px; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:640px; background:rgb(244,247,249)"></a></p>
<span id="OSC_h2_20" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"></span>
<h2 style="padding:0px; margin:20px 0px 10px; line-height:36px; font-size:20px">9.<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">删除条目</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">delete</span></h2>
<p style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; letter-spacing:0.5px; font-size:12.5px">
<a target="_blank" href="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163628_yvnw_256028.png" rel="nofollow" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:rgb(255,131,115); outline:0px; font-size:12px"><img src="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163628_yvnw_256028.png" alt="" style="padding:5px; margin:10px 0px; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:640px; background:rgb(244,247,249)"></a><br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
<br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">清空表：<br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
</span><a target="_blank" href="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163638_4XWD_256028.png" rel="nofollow" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:rgb(255,131,115); outline:0px; font-size:12px"><img src="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163638_4XWD_256028.png" alt="" style="padding:5px; margin:10px 0px; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:640px; background:rgb(244,247,249)"></a><br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
<br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">truncate</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">是一个能够快速清空资料表内所有资料的</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">SQL</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">语法。并且能针对具有自动递增值的字段，做计数重置归零重新计算的作用<br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
<br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
</span></p>
<span id="OSC_h2_21" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"></span>
<h2 style="padding:0px; margin:20px 0px 10px; line-height:36px; font-size:20px">10.<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">统计参数</span></h2>
<p style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; letter-spacing:0.5px; font-size:12.5px">
<a target="_blank" href="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163649_ldIm_256028.png" rel="nofollow" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:rgb(255,131,115); outline:0px; font-size:12px"><img src="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163649_ldIm_256028.png" alt="" style="padding:5px; margin:10px 0px; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:640px; background:rgb(244,247,249)"></a></p>
<span id="OSC_h1_22" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"></span>
<h1 style="padding:0px; margin:20px 0px 10px; line-height:43.2000007629395px; font-size:24px">
三。<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">JavaAPI</span></h1>
<p style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:8px; margin-bottom:8px; letter-spacing:0.5px; font-size:12.5px">
全部<span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">API</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">在</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">%HBase%/docs</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px">目录里，完全是英文的。<br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">本例所须全部</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">jar</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">都可以在</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">%HBase</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">安装目录</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">%/lib</span><span style="padding:0px; margin:0px; line-height:1.5; font-size:12.5px">目录中找到。图省事，我一股脑儿全导入了。<br style="padding:0px; margin:0px">
</span><a target="_blank" href="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163657_4kY0_256028.png" rel="nofollow" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:rgb(255,131,115); outline:0px; font-size:12px"><img src="http://static.oschina.net/uploads/space/2014/0403/163657_4kY0_256028.png" alt="" style="padding:5px; margin:10px 0px; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:640px; background:rgb(244,247,249)"></a></p>
